CHAPTER XXX BLACKY THE CROW IS ALL PITY People who think that they be fool others very often discover that they have be fool themselves .
Bowser the Hound .
To have see and hear Blacky the Crow a he talk to Reddy Fox , you would have think that there be nothing under the sun in his heart or mind but pity .
`` Yes , Sir , '' say he , `` I certainly would be tempt to show you where those fat hen be if you be not too weak .
I just ca n't bear to see an old friend starve .
It be too bad that those fat hen be so far away .
I feel sure that one of them would make you quite yourself again . ''
`` Do n't -- do n't talk about them , '' say Reddy feebly .
`` If I could have just one fat hen that be all I would ask .
Are they so very far from here ? ''
Blacky nod his head vigorously .
`` Yes , '' say he , `` they be a long way from here .
They be such a long way that I 'm afraid you be too weak to make the journey .
If you be quite yourself you could do it nicely , but for one in your condition it be , I fear , altogether too long a journey . ''
`` It would n't do any harm to try it , perhaps , '' suggest Reddy , in a hesitating way .
`` It be no bad to starve to death in one place than another , and I never be one to give up without try .
If you do n't mind show me the way , Brother Blacky , I would at least like to try to reach that place where the fat hen be .
Of course I can not keep up with you .
In fact , I could n't if I be feel well and strong .
Perhaps you can tell me just how to find that place , and then I need n't bother you at all . ''
Blacky pretend to be lose in thought while Reddy watch him anxiously .
Finally Blacky speak .
`` It certainly make my heart ache to see you in such a condition , Brother Reddy , '' say he .
`` I tell you what I 'll do .
You know Crows be famous for fly in a straight line when we want to get to any place in particular .
I will fly straight towards that farm where the fat hen be .
You follow along as best you can .
In your feeble condition it will take you a long time to get anywhere near there .
This will give me time to go hunt for my own dinner , and then I will come back until I meet you .
After that , I will show you the way .
Now I will start along and you follow . ''
Reddy get to his foot a if it be hard work .
Then Blacky spread his wing and start off , caw encouragement .
All the time inside he be laugh to think that Reddy Fox should think he have fool him .
`` He forget to ask again if there be a dog there , '' chuckle Blacky to himself .
As for Reddy , no sooner be Blacky well on his way than he start off at his swift pace .
There be nothing weak or feeble in the way Reddy run then .
He be in a hurry to get to those fat hen .
CHAPTER XXXI BLACKY IS MUCH PLEASED WITH HIMSELF You can not tell from a single feather what a bird look like , nor from a lone hair how big a dog be .
Bowser the Hound .
Straight away towards the farm where Bowser the Hound be flew Blacky the Crow .
Every few minute he would caw encouragement to Reddy Fox , who , a you know , be follow , but who of course could not travel as fast a do Blacky .
In between time Blacky would chuckle to himself .
He be mightily pleased with himself , be Blacky .
In the first place his plan be work beautifully .
You know what he be after be to get Reddy Fox over to that farm where Bowser be .
He hop that if Reddy should catch one of those fat hen , the farmer would put Bowser on Reddy 's trail .
He know that Reddy would probably return straight home , and Bowser , follow Reddy 's trail , would thus find his way back home to Farmer Brown 's .
Of course , it all depend on whether Reddy would catch one of those fat hen and whether Bowser would be allow to hunt him .

But what tickle Blacky most the knowledge that Reddy Fox think he be fool Blacky .

There be nothing weak or feeble in the way that red speck be come across the snow-covered field .
Blacky chuckle hoarsely .

Presently it stop move fast .
It begin to move slowly and stop every once in a while , a if to rest .
Blacky laugh right out .
He know then that Reddy Fox have discover him sit in the top of that tall tree and be once more pretending .
It be a sort of a game , a game that Blacky thoroughly enjoy .
As soon a he know that Reddy have discover him , he once more spread his black wing and start on .

In fact , Blacky do not fly far this time before once more waiting .
It be great fun to see Reddy suddenly pretend that he be too weak to run .
It be such fun that Blacky quite forget that he have have no breakfast .
Yes , Blacky the Crow be very much please with himself .
It look very much a if he would succeed in help Bowser the Hound .
This please him .
But it please him still more to know that he be fool clever Reddy Fox while Reddy think he be the one who be do the fooling .
CHAPTER XXXII BLACKY WAITS FOR REDDY Be wise , my friend , and do not fail To trust a dog who wag his tail .
Bowser the Hound .
Just before reach the farm where the fat hen and Bowser the Hound be , Blacky wait for Reddy Fox to catch up .

It be a noiseless chuckle , for Blacky do not intend to give himself away until he have to .

`` You must excuse me for keep you wait , but I do not suppose that any one so weak and feeble a you appear to be early this morning could possibly get here so soon . ''

`` The thought of those fat hen have quite restore my strength .
Did you say that they be near here ? ''
`` I do n't say , but -- '' Blacky do n't finish .
He do n't need to .

`` Are you satisfy that I tell the truth ? ''

CHAPTER XXXIII REDDY WATCHES THE FAT HENS Sooner or later the crooked trail will straighten .
Bowser the Hound .

CHAPTER XXXIV PATIENCE AND IMPATIENCE Patience be a virtue In a cause that 's right .
In a cause that be n't , It 's a cause for fright .
Bowser the Hound .

CHAPTER XXXVI REDDY HIDES THE FAT HEN Dishonesty will run away Where Honesty will boldly stay .

CHAPTER XL WHERE WAS REDDY 'S DINNER ?
Often it be well to look for a new trail than to waste time hunt for an old one .
Bowser the Hound .

CHAPTER XLI WHAT BLACKY THE CROW SAW The great puzzle be simple enough when you know the answer .

CHAPTER XLII ALL IS WELL THAT ENDS WELL When thing go wrong , just patient be Until the end you plainly see .

Bowser the Hound .

CHAPTER I : Peter Rabbit Meets Lightfoot Peter Rabbit be on his way back from the pond of Paddy the Beaver deep in the Green Forest .
He have just see Mr. and Mrs. Quack start toward the Big River for a brief visit before leave on their long , difficult journey to the far-away Southland .
Farewells be always rather sad , and this particular farewell have leave Peter with a lump in his throat , -- a queer , choky feeling .
`` If I be sure that they would return next spring , it would n't be so bad , '' he mutter .
`` It 's those terrible gun .
I know what it be to have to watch out for them .
Farmer Brown 's boy use to hunt me with one of them , but he do n't any more .
But even when he do hunt me it be n't anything like what the Ducks have to go through .
If I keep my eye and ear open , I could tell when a hunter be come and could hide in a hole if I want to .
I never have to worry about my meal .
But with the Ducks it be a thousand time worse .
They 've get to eat while make that long journey , and they can eat only where there be the right kind of food .
Hunters with terrible gun know where those place be and hide there until the Ducks come , and the Ducks have no way of know whether the hunter be wait for them or not .
That be n't hunt .
It 's -- it 's -- '' `` Well , what be it ?
What be you talk to yourself about , Peter Rabbit ? ''
Peter look up with a start to find the soft , beautiful eye of Lightfoot the Deer gaze down at him over the top of a little hemlock tree .
`` It 's awful , '' declare Peter .
`` It 's bad than unfair .
It do n't give them any chance at all . ''
`` I suppose it must be so if you say so , '' reply Lightfoot , `` but you might tell me what all this awfulness be about . ''
Peter grin .
Then he begin at the beginning and tell Lightfoot all about Mr. and Mrs. Quack and the many danger they must face on their long journey to the far-away Southland and back again in the spring , all because of the heartless hunter with terrible gun .
Lightfoot listen and his great soft eye be fill with pity for the Quack family .
`` I hope they will get through all right , '' say he , `` and I hope they will get back in the spring .
It be bad enough to be hunt by men at one time of the year , a no one know good than I do , but to be hunt in the spring as well a in the fall be more than twice a bad .
Men be strange creature .
I do not understand them at all .
None of the people of the Green Forest would think of do such terrible thing .
I suppose it be quite right to hunt others in order to get enough to eat , though I be thankful to say that I never have have to do that , but to hunt others just for the fun of hunting be something I can not understand at all .
And yet that be what men seem to do it for .
I guess the trouble be they never have be hunt themselves and do n't know how it feel .
Sometimes I think I 'll hunt one some day just to teach him a lesson .
What be you laugh at , Peter ? ''
`` At the idea of you hunt a man , '' reply Peter .
`` Your heart be all right , Lightfoot , but you be too timid and gentle to frighten any one .
Big a you be I would n't fear you . ''
With a single swift bound Lightfoot spring out in front of Peter .
He stamp his sharp hoof , lower his handsome head until the sharp point of his antler , which people call horn , point straight at Peter , lift the hair along the back of his neck , and make a motion a if to plunge at him .
His eye , which Peter have always think so soft and gentle , seem to flash fire .
`` Oh ! ''
cry Peter in a faint , frightened-sounding voice and leap to one side before it enter his foolish little head that Lightfoot be just pretend .
Lightfoot chuckle .
`` Did you say I could n't frighten any one ? ''
he demand .
`` I -- I do n't know you could look so terribly fierce , '' stammer Peter .
`` Those antler look really dangerous when you point them that way .
Why -- why -- what be that hang to them ?
It look like bit of old fur .
Have you be tear somebody 's coat , Lightfoot ? ''
Peter 's eye be wide with wonder and suspicion .
CHAPTER II : Lightfoot 's New Antlers Peter Rabbit be puzzle .
He star at Lightfoot the Deer a wee bit suspiciously .
`` Have you be tear somebody 's coat ? ''
he ask again .
He do n't like to think it of Lightfoot , whom he always have believe quite a gentle , harmless , and timid a himself .
But what else could he think ?
Lightfoot slowly shake his head .
`` No , '' say he , `` I have n't tear anybody 's coat . ''
`` Then what be those rag hang on your antler ? ''
demand Peter .
Lightfoot chuckle .
`` They be what be leave of the covering of my new antler , '' he explain .
`` What 's that ?
What do you mean by new antler ? ''
Peter be sit up very straight , with his eye fix on Lightfoot 's antler a though he never have see them before .
`` Just what I say , '' retort Lightfoot .
`` What do you think of them ?
I think they be the fine antler I 've ever have .
When I get the rest of those rag off , they will be a handsome a set a ever be grow in the Green Forest . ''
Lightfoot rub his antler against the trunk of a tree till some of the rag hang to them drop off .
Peter blink very hard .
He be try to understand and he could n't .
Finally he say so .
`` What kind of a story be you try to fill me up with ? ''
he demand indignantly .
`` Do you mean to tell me that those be not the antler that you have have as long a I 've know you ?
How can anything hard like those antler grow ?
And if those be new one , where be the old one ?
Show me the old one , and perhaps I 'll believe that these be new one .
The idea of try to make me believe that antler grow just like plant !
I 've see Bossy the Cow all summer and I know she have get the same horn she have last summer .
New antler indeed ! ''
`` You be quite right , Peter , quite right about Bossy the Cow .
She never have new horn , but that be n't any reason why I should n't have new antler , be it ? ''
replied Lightfoot patiently .
`` Her horn be quite different from my antler .
I have a new pair every year .
You have n't see me all summer , have you , Peter ? ''
`` No , I do n't remember that I have , '' reply Peter , try very hard to remember when he have last see Lightfoot .
`` I KNOW you have n't , '' retort Lightfoot .
`` I know it because I have be hide in a place you never visit . ''
`` What have you be hide for ? ''
demand Peter .
`` For my new antler to grow , '' reply Lightfoot .
`` When my new antler be grow , I want to be away by myself .
I do n't like to be see without them or with halfgrown one .
Besides , I be very uncomfortable while the new antler be grow and I want to be alone . ''
Lightfoot speak a if he really mean every word he say , but still Peter could n't , he just COULD N'T believe that those wonderful great antler have grow out of Lightfoot 's head in a single summer .
`` Where do you leave your old one and when do they come off ? ''
he ask , and there be doubt in the very tone of his voice .
`` They drop off last spring , but I do n't remember just where , '' reply Lightfoot .
`` I be too glad to be rid of them to notice where they drop .
You see they be loose and uncomfortable , and I have n't any more use for them because I know that my new one would be big and well .
I 've get one more point on each than I have last year . ''
Lightfoot begin once more to rub his antler against the tree to get off the queer rag hang to them and to polish the point .
Peter watch in silence for a few minute .
Then , all his suspicion return , he say : `` But you have n't tell me anything about those rag hang to your antler . ''
`` And you have n't believe what I have already tell you , '' retort Lightfoot .
`` I do n't like tell thing to people who wo n't believe me . ''
CHAPTER III : Lightfoot Tells How His Antlers Grew It be hard to believe what seem impossible .
And yet what seem impossible to you may be a very commonplace matter to some one else .
So it do not do to say that a thing can not be possible just because you can not understand how it can be .
Peter Rabbit want to believe what Lightfoot the Deer have just tell him , but somehow he could n't .
If he have see those antler grow , it would have be another matter .
But he have n't see Lightfoot since the very last of winter , and then Lightfoot have wear just such handsome antler a he now have .
So Peter really could n't be blame for not be able to believe that those old one have be lose and in their place new one have grow in just the few month of spring and summer .
But Peter do n't blame Lightfoot in the least , because he have tell Peter that he do n't like to tell thing to people who would n't believe what he tell them when Peter have ask him about the rag hang to his antler .
`` I 'm try to believe it , '' he say , quite humbly .
`` It 's all true , '' break in another voice .
Peter jump and turn to find his big cousin , Jumper the Hare .
Unseen and unheard , he have steal up and have overhear what Peter and Lightfoot have say .
`` How do you know it be true ? ''
snap Peter a little crossly , for Jumper have startle him .
`` Because I saw Lightfoot 's old antler after they have fall off , and I often saw Lightfoot while his new one be grow , '' retort Jumper .
`` All right !
I 'll believe anything that Lightfoot tell me if you say it be true , '' declare Peter , who greatly admire his cousin , Jumper .
`` Now tell me about those rag , Lightfoot .
Please do . ''
Lightfoot could n't resist that `` please . ''
`` Those rag be what be leave of a kind of cover which protect the antler while they be grow , a I tell you before , '' say he .
`` Very soon after my old one drop off the new one begin to grow .
They be not hard , not at all like they be now .
They be soft and very tender , and the blood run through them just a it do through our body .
They be cover with a sort of skin with hair on it like thin fur .
The end be not sharply point they now be , but be big and round , like knob .
They be not like antler at all , and they make my head hot and be very uncomfortable .
That be why I hide away .
They grow very fast , so fast that every day I could see by look at my reflection in water that they be a little long .
It seem to me sometimes a if all my strength go into those new antler .
And I have to be very careful not to hit them against anything .
In the first place it would have hurt , and in the second place it might have spoil the shape of them .
`` When they have grow to the length you now see , they begin to shrink and grow hard .
The knob on the end shrink until they become point .
As soon a they stop grow the blood stop flow up in them , and a they become hard they be no long tender .
The skin which have cover them grow dry and split , and I rub it off on tree and bush .
The little rag you see be what be leave , but I will soon be rid of those .
Then I shall be ready to fight if need be and will fear no one save man , and will fear him only when he have a terrible gun with him . ''
Lightfoot toss his head proudly and rattle his wonderful antler against the near tree .
`` Is n't he handsome , '' whisper Peter to Jumper the Hare ; `` and do you ever hear of anything so wonderful a the growing of those new antler in such a short time ?
It be hard to believe , but I suppose it must be true . ''
`` It be , '' reply Jumper , `` and I tell you , Peter , I would hate to have Lightfoot try those antler on me , even though I be big a a man .
You 've always think of Lightfoot a timid and afraid , but you should see him when he be angry .
Few people care to face him then . ''
CHAPTER IV : The Spirit Of Fear When the day grow cold and the night be clear , There stalk abroad the spirit of fear .
-- Lightfoot the Deer .
It be sad but true .
Autumn be often call the sad time of the year , and it be the sad time .
But it should n't be .
Old Mother Nature never intend that it should be .
She mean it to be the GLAD time .
It be the time when all the little people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows have get over the care and worry of bring up family and teach their child how to look out for themselves .
It be the season when food be plentiful , and every one be fat and be , or ought to be , care free .
It be the season when Old Mother Nature intend all her little people to be happy , to have nothing to worry them for the little time before the come of cold weather and the hard time which cold weather always bring .
But instead of this , a grim , dark figure go stalk over the Green Meadows and through the Green Forest , and it be call the Spirit of Fear .
It peer into every hiding-place and wherever it find one of the little people it send little cold chill over him , little chill which jolly , round , bright Mr. Sun can not chase away , though he shine his bright .
All night as well a all day the Spirit of Fear search out the little people of the Green Meadows and the Green Forest .
It will not let them sleep .
It will not let them eat in peace .
It drive them to seek new hiding-places and then drive them out of those .
It keep them ever ready to fly or run at the slight sound .
Peter Rabbit be think of this a he sit at the edge of the dear Old Briar-patch , look over to the Green Forest .
The Green Forest be no longer just green ; it be of many color , for Old Mother Nature have set Jack Frost to paint the leaf of the maple-trees and the beech-trees , and the birch-trees and the poplar-trees and the chestnut-trees , and he have do his work well .
Very , very lovely be the red and yellow and brown against the dark green of the pine and the spruce and the hemlock .
The Purple Hills be more softly purple than at any other season of the year .
It be all very , very beautiful .
But Peter have no thought for the beauty of it all , for the Spirit of Fear have visit even the dear Old Briar-patch , and Peter be afraid .
It be n't fear of Reddy Fox , or Redtail the Hawk , or Hooty the Owl , or Old Man Coyote .
They be forever try to catch him , but they do not strike terror to his heart because he felt quite smart enough to keep out of their clutch .
To be sure , they give him sudden fright sometimes , when they happen to surprise him , but these fright last only until he reach the near bramble-tangle or hollow log where they could not get at him .
But the fear that chill his heart now never leave him even for a moment .
And Peter know that this same fear be clutch at the heart of Bob White , hiding in the brown stubble ; of Mrs. Grouse , squat in the thick bramble-tangle in the Green Forest ; of Uncle Billy Possum and Bobby Coon in their hollow tree ; of Jerry Muskrat in the Smiling Pool ; of Happy Jack Squirrel , hide in the tree top ; of Lightfoot the Deer , lie in the closest thicket he could find .
It be even clutch at the heart of Granny and Reddy Fox and of great , big Buster Bear .
It seem to Peter that no one be so big or so small that this terrible Spirit of Fear have not search him out .
Far in the distance sound a sudden bang .
Peter jump and shiver .
He know that every one else who have hear that bang have jump and shiver just a he have .
It be the season of hunter with terrible gun .
It be man who have send this terrible Spirit of Fear to chill the heart of the little meadow and forest people at this very time when Old Mother Nature have make all thing so beautiful and have intend that they should be happiest and most free from care and worry .
It be man who have make the autumn a sad time instead of a glad time , the very sad time of all the year , when Old Mother Nature have do her best to make it the most beautiful .
`` I do n't understand these men creature , '' say Peter to little Mrs. Peter , a they star fearfully out from the dear Old Briar-patch .
`` They seem to find pleasure , actually find pleasure , in try to kill u .
I do n't understand them at all .
They have n't any heart .
That must be the reason ; they have n't any heart . ''
CHAPTER V : Sammy Jay Brings Lightfoot Word Sammy Jay be one of those who believe in the wisdom of the old saying , `` Early to bed and early to rise . ''
Sammy need no alarm clock to get up early in the morning .
He be awake as soon a it be light enough to see and waste no time wish he could sleep a little long .
His stomach would n't let him if he want to .
Sammy always wake up hungry .
In this he be no different from all his feathered neighbor .
So the minute Sammy get his eye open he make his toilet , for Sammy be very neat , and start out to hunt for his breakfast .
Long ago Sammy discover that there be no safe time of day to visit the dooryard of those two-legged creature call men than very early in the morning .
On this particular morning he have plan to fly over to Farmer Brown 's dooryard , but at the last minute he change his mind .
Instead , he fly over to the dooryard of another farm .
It be so very early in the morning that Sammy do n't expect to find anybody stirring , so you can guess how surprised he be when , just a he come in sight of that dooryard , he saw the door of the house open and a man step out .
Sammy stop on the top of the near tree .
`` Now what be that man do up as early a this ? ''
mutter Sammy .
Then he catch sight of something under the man 's arm .
He do n't have to look twice to know what it be .
It be a gun !
Yes , sir , it be a gun , a terrible gun .
`` Ha ! ''
exclaim Sammy , and quite forget that his stomach be empty .
`` Now who can that fellow be after so early in the morning ?
I wonder if he be go to the dear Old Briar-patch to look for Peter Rabbit , or if he be go to the Old Pasture in search of Reddy Fox , or if it be Mr. and Mrs. Grouse he hop to kill .
I think I 'll sit right here and watch . ''
So Sammy sit in the top of the tree and watch the hunter with the terrible gun .
He saw him head straight for the Green Forest .
`` It 's Mr. and Mrs. Grouse after all , I guess , '' think Sammy .
`` If I know just where they be I 'd go over and warn them . ''
But Sammy do n't know just where they be and he know that it might take him a long time to find them , so he once more begin to think of breakfast and then , right then , another thought pop into his head .
He think of Lightfoot the Deer .
Sammy watch the hunter enter the Green Forest , then he silently follow him .
From the way the hunter move , Sammy decide that he be n't think of Mr. and Mrs. Grouse .
`` It 's Lightfoot the Deer , sure a I live , '' mutter Sammy .
`` He ought to be warn .
He certainly ought to be warn .
I know right where he be .
I believe I 'll warn him myself . ''
Sammy find Lightfoot right where he have expect to .
`` He 's come ! ''
cry Sammy .
`` A hunter with a terrible gun be come ! ''
CHAPTER VI : A Game Of Hide And Seek There be a game of hide and seek that Danny Meadow Mouse once play with Buster Bear .
It be a very dreadful game for Danny .
But hard a it be for Danny , it do n't begin to be as hard a the game Lightfoot the Deer be play with the hunter in the Green Forest .
In the case of Buster Bear and Danny , the latter have simply to keep out of reach of Buster .
As long a Buster do n't get his great paw on Danny , the latter be safe .
Then , too , Danny be a very small person .
He be so small that he can hide under two or three leaf .
Wherever he be , he be pretty sure to find a hiding-place of some sort .
His small size give him advantage in a game of hide and seek .
It certainly do .
But Lightfoot the Deer be big .
He be one of the large of the people who live in the Green Forest .
Being so big , it be not easy to hide .
Moreover , a hunter with a terrible gun do not have to get close in order to kill .
Lightfoot know all this a he wait for the come of the hunter of whom Sammy Jay have warn him .
He have learn many lesson in the hunting season of the year before and he remember every one of them .
He know that to forget even one of them might cost him his life .
So , stand motionless behind a tangle of fall tree , Lightfoot listen and watch .
Presently over in the distance he hear Sammy Jay screaming , `` Thief , thief , thief ! ''
A little sigh of relief escape Lightfoot .
He know that that screaming of Sammy Jay 's be a warning to tell him where the hunter be .
Knowing just where the hunter be make it easy for Lightfoot to know what to do .
A Merry Little Breeze come steal through the Green Forest .
It come from behind Lightfoot and dance on towards the hunter with the terrible gun .
Instantly Lightfoot begin to steal softly away through the Green Forest .
He take the great care to make no sound .
He go in a half-circle , stop every few step to listen and test the air with his wonderful nose .
Can you guess what Lightfoot be try to do ?
He be try to get behind the hunter so that the Merry Little Breezes would bring to him the dread man-scent .
So long a Lightfoot could get that scent , he would know where the hunter be , though he could neither see nor hear him .
If he have remain where Sammy Jay have find him , the hunter might have come within shoot distance before Lightfoot could have locate him .
So the hunter with the terrible gun walk noiselessly through the Green Forest , step with the great care to avoid snap a stick underfoot , search with keen eye every thicket and likely hiding-place for a glimpse of Lightfoot , and study the ground for trace to show that Lightfoot have be there .
CHAPTER VII : The Merry Little Breezes Help Lightfoot Could you have see the hunter with the terrible gun and Lightfoot the Deer that morning on which the hunting season open you might have think that Lightfoot be hunt the hunter instead of the hunter hunt Lightfoot .
You see , Lightfoot be behind the hunter instead of in front of him .
He be follow the hunter , so a to keep track of him .
As long a he know just where the hunter be , he felt reasonably safe .
The Merry Little Breezes be Lightfoot 's best friend .
They always bring to him all the different scent they find a they wander through the Green Forest .
And Lightfoot 's delicate nose be so wonderful that he can take these scent , even though they be very faint , and tell just who or what have make them .
So , though he make the best possible use of his big ear and his beautiful eye , he trust more to his nose to warn him of danger .
For this reason , during the hunting season when he move about , he move in the direction from which the Merry Little Breezes may be blow .
He know that they will bring to him warn of any danger which may lie in that direction .
Now the hunter with the terrible gun who be look for Lightfoot know all this , for he be wise in the way of Lightfoot and of the other little people of the Green Forest .
When he have enter the Green Forest that morning he have first of all make sure of the direction from which the Merry Little Breezes be come .
Then he have begin to hunt in that direction , know that thus his scent would be carry behind him .
It be more than likely that he would have reach the hiding-place of Lightfoot the Deer before the latter would have know that he be in the Green Forest , have it not be for Sammy Jay 's warning .
When he reach the tangle of fall tree behind which Lightfoot have be hide , he work around it slowly and with the great care , hold his terrible gun ready to use instantly should Lightfoot leap out .
Presently he find Lightfoot 's footprint in the soft ground and study them he know that Lightfoot have know of his come .
`` It be that confound Jay , '' mutter the hunter .
`` Lightfoot hear him and know what it mean .
I know what he have do ; he have circle round so a to get behind me and get my scent .
It be a clever trick , a very clever trick , but two can play at that game .
I 'll just try that little trick myself . ''
So the hunter in his turn make a wide circle back , and presently there be none of the dreaded man-smell among the scent which the Merry Little Breezes bring to Lightfoot .
Lightfoot have lose track of the hunter .
CHAPTER VIII : Wit Against Wit It be a dreadful game the hunter with the terrible gun and Lightfoot the Deer be play in the Green Forest .
It be a matching of wit against wit , the hunter seek to take Lightfoot 's life , and Lightfoot seek to save it .
The experience of other year have teach Lightfoot much of the way of hunter and not one of the thing he have learn about them be forget .
But the hunter in his turn know much of the way of Deer .
So it be that each be try his best to outguess the other .
When the hunter find the hiding-place Lightfoot have leave at the warning of Sammy Jay he follow Lightfoot 's track for a short distance .
It be slow work , and only one whose eye have be train to notice little thing could have do it .
You see , there be no snow , and only now and then , when he have step on a bit of soft ground , have Lightfoot leave a footprint .
But there be other sign which the hunter know how to read , -- a freshly upturned leaf here , and here , a bit of moss lightly crush .
These thing tell the hunter which way Lightfoot have go .
Slowly , patiently , watchfully , the hunter follow .
After a while he stop with a satisfied grin .
`` I think as much , '' he mutter .
`` He hear that pesky Jay and circle around so a to get my scent .
I 'll just cut across to my old trail and unless I be greatly mistaken , I 'll find his track there . ''
So , swiftly but silently , the hunter cut across to his old trail , and in a few moment he find just what he expect , -- one of Lightfoot 's footprint .
Once more he grin .
`` Well , old fellow , I 've outguess you this time , '' say he to himself .
`` I be behind you and the wind be from you to me , so that you can not get my scent .
I would n't be a bit surprised if you 're back right where you start from , behind that old windfall . ''
He at once begin to move forward silently and cautiously , with eye and ear alert and his terrible gun ready for instant use .
Now when Lightfoot , follow behind the hunter , have lose the scent of the latter , he guess right away that the latter have find his track and have start to follow them .
Lightfoot stand still and listen with all his might for some little sound to tell him where the hunter be .
But there be no sound and after a little Lightfoot begin to move on .
He do n't dare remain still , l the hunter should creep up within shoot distance .
There be only one direction in which it be safe for Lightfoot to move , and that be the direction from which the Merry Little Breezes be blow .
So long a they bring him none of the dreaded man-smell , he know that he be safe .
The hunter might be behind him -- probably he be -- but ahead of him , so long a the Merry Little Breezes be blow in his face and bring no man-smell , be safety .
CHAPTER IX : Lightfoot Becomes Uncertain Lightfoot the Deer travel on through the Green Forest , straight ahead in the direction from which the Merry Little Breezes be blow .
Every few step he would raise his delicate nose and test all the scent that the Merry Little Breezes be bring .
So long a he keep the Merry Little Breezes blow in his face , he could be sure whether or not there be danger ahead of him .
Lightfoot use his nose very much a you and I use our eye .
It tell him the thing he want to know .
He know that Reddy Fox have be along ahead of him , although he do n't get so much a a glimpse of Reddy 's red coat .
Once he catch just the faint of scent which cause him to stop abruptly and test the air more carefully than ever .
It be the scent of Buster Bear .
But it be so very faint that Lightfoot know Buster be not near , so he go ahead again , but even more carefully than before .
After a little he could n't smell Buster at all , so he know then that Buster have merely pass that way when he be go to some other part of the Green Forest .
Lightfoot know that he have nothing to fear in that direction so long a the Merry Little Breezes bring him none of the dreaded man-scent , and he know that he could trust the Merry Little Breezes to bring him that scent if there should be a man anywhere in front of him .
You know the Merry Little Breezes be Lightfoot 's best friend .
But Lightfoot do n't want to keep go in that direction all day .
It would take him far away from that part of the Green Forest with which he be familiar and which he call home .
It might in time take him out of the Green Forest and that would n't do at all .
So after a while Lightfoot become uncertain .
He do n't know just what to do .
You see , he could n't tell whether or not that hunter with the terrible gun be still follow him .
Every once in a while he would stop in a thicket of young tree or behind a tangle of fall tree uproot by the wind .
There he would stand , face the direction from which he have come , and watch and listen for some sign that the hunter be still follow .
But after a few minute of this he would grow uneasy and then bind away in the direction from which the Merry Little Breezes be blow , so a to be sure of not run into danger .
`` If only I could know if that hunter be still follow , I would know good what to do , '' think Lightfoot .
`` I 've get to find out . ''
CHAPTER X : Lightfoot 's Clever Trick Lightfoot the Deer be smart .
Yes , Sir , Lightfoot the Deer be smart .
He have to be , especially in the hunting season , to save his life .
If he be not smart he would have be kill long ago .
He never make the foolish mistake of thinking that other people be not smart .
He know that the hunter who have start out to follow him early that morning be not one to be easily discourage or to be fool by simple trick .
He have a very great respect for the smartness of that hunter .
He know that he could n't afford to be careless for one little minute .
The certainty of danger be sometimes easy to bear than the uncertainty of not know whether or not there really be any danger .
Lightfoot felt that if he could know just where the hunter be , he himself would know good what to do .
The hunter might have become discouraged and give up follow him .
In that case he could rest and stop worrying .
It would be good to know that he be be follow than not to know .
But how be he to find out ?
Lightfoot keep turn this over and over in his mind a he travel through the Green Forest .
Then an idea come to him .
`` I know what I 'll do .
I know just what I 'll do , '' say Lightfoot to himself .
`` I 'll find out whether or not that hunter be still follow me and I 'll get a little rest .
Goodness know , I need a rest . ''
Lightfoot bound away swiftly and run for some distance , then he turn and quickly , but very , very quietly , return in the direction from which he have just come but a little to one side of his old trail .
After a while he saw what he be look for , a pile of branch which woodchoppers have leave when they have trim the tree they have cut down .
This be near the top of a little hill .
Lightfoot go up the hill and stop behind the pile of brush .
For a few moment he stand there perfectly still , look and listen .
Then , with a little sigh of relief , he lay down , where , without be in any danger of be see himself , he could watch his old trail through the hollow at the bottom of the hill .
If the hunter be still follow him , he would pass through that hollow in plain sight .
For a long tune Lightfoot rest comfortably behind the pile of brush .
There be not a suspicious movement or a suspicious sound to show that danger be abroad in the Green Forest .
He saw Mr. and Mrs. Grouse fly down across the hollow and disappear among the tree on the other side .
He saw Unc ' Billy Possum look over a hollow tree and guess that Unc ' Billy be get ready to go into winter quarter .
He saw Jumper the Hare squat down under a low-hanging branch of a hemlock-tree and prepare to take a nap .
He hear Drummer the Woodpecker at work drilling after worm in a tree not far away .
Little by little Lightfoot grow easy in his mind .
It must be that that hunter have become discouraged and be no longer follow him .
CHAPTER XI : The Hunted Watches The Hunter It be so quiet and peaceful and altogether lovely there in the Green Forest , where Lightfoot the Deer lay rest behind a pile of brush near the top of a little hill , that it do n't seem possible such a thing a sudden death could be anywhere near .
It do n't seem possible that there could be any need for watchfulness .
But Lightfoot long ago have learn that often danger be near when it seem least to be expect .
So , though he would have like very much to have take a nap , Lightfoot be too wise to do anything so foolish .
He keep his beautiful , great , soft eye fix in the direction from which the hunter with the terrible gun would come if he be still follow that trail .
He keep his great ear gently move to catch every little sound .
Lightfoot have about decide that the hunter have give up hunt for that day , but he do n't let this keep him from be any the less watchful .
It be well to be overwatchful than the least bit careless .
By and by , Lightfoot 's keen ear catch the sound of the snapping of a little stick in the distance .
It be so faint a sound that you or I would have miss it altogether .
But Lightfoot hear it and instantly he be doubly alert , watch in the direction from which that faint sound have come .
After what seem a long , long time he saw something moving , and a moment later a man come into view .
It be the hunter and across one arm he carry the terrible gun .
Lightfoot know now that this hunter have patience and perseverance and have not yet give up hope of get near enough to shoot Lightfoot .
He move forward slowly , set each foot down with the great care , so a not to snap a stick or rustle the leaf .
He be watch sharply ahead , ready to shoot should he catch a glimpse of Lightfoot within range .
Right along through the hollow at the foot of the little hill below Lightfoot the hunter pass .
He be no longer study the ground for Lightfoot 's track , because the ground be so hard and dry down there that Lightfoot have leave no track .
He be simply hunt in the direction from which the Merry Little Breezes be blow because he know that Lightfoot have go in that direction , and he also know that if Lightfoot be still ahead of him , his scent could not be carry to Lightfoot .
He be do what be call `` hunting up-wind . ''
Lightfoot keep perfectly still and watch the hunter disappear among the tree .
Then he silently get to his foot , shake himself lightly , and noiselessly stole away over the hilltop towards another part of the Green Forest .
He felt sure that that hunter would not find him again that day .
CHAPTER XII : Lightfoot Visits Paddy The Beaver Deep in the Green Forest be the pond where live Paddy the Beaver .
It be Paddy 's own pond , for he make it himself .
He make it by build a dam across the Laughing Brook .
When Lightfoot bound away through the Green Forest , after watch the hunter pas through the hollow below him , he remember Paddy 's pond .
`` That 's where I 'll go , '' think Lightfoot .
`` It be such a lonesome part of the Green Forest that I do not believe that hunter will come there .
I 'll just run over and make Paddy a friendly call . ''
So Lightfoot bound along deep and deeply into the Green Forest .
Presently through the tree he catch the gleam of water .
It be Paddy 's pond .
Lightfoot approach it cautiously .
He felt sure he be rid of the hunter who have follow him so far that day , but he know that there might be other hunter in the Green Forest .
He know that he could n't afford to be careless for even one little minute .
Lightfoot have live long enough to know that most of the sad thing and dreadful thing that happen in the Green Forest and on the Green Meadows be due to carelessness .
No one who be hunt , be he big or little , can afford ever to be careless .
Now Lightfoot have know of hunter hide near water , hop to shoot him when he come to drink .
That always seem to Lightfoot a dreadful thing , an unfair thing .
But hunter have do it before and they might do it again .
So Lightfoot be careful to approach Paddy 's pond upwind .
That be , he approach the side of the pond from which the Merry Little Breezes be blow toward him , and all the time he keep his nose working .
He know that if any hunter be hide there , the Merry Little Breezes would bring him their scent and thus warn him .
He have almost reach the edge of Paddy 's pond when from the farther shore there come a sudden crash .
It startle Lightfoot terribly for just an instant .
Then he guess what it mean .
That crash be the fall of a tree .
There be n't enough wind to blow over even the most shaky dead tree .
There have be no sound of ax , so he know it could not have be chop down by men .
It must be that Paddy the Beaver have cut it , and if Paddy have be work in daylight , it be certain that no one have be around that pond for a long time .
So Lightfoot hurry forward eagerly , cautiously .
When he reach the bank he look across towards where the sound of that fall tree have come from ; a branch of a tree be move along in the water and half hide by it be a brown head .
It be Paddy the Beaver take the branch to his food pile .
CHAPTER XIII : Lightfoot And Paddy Become Partners The instant Lightfoot saw Paddy the Beaver he know that for the time be , at least , there be no danger .
He know that Paddy be one of the shy of all the little people of the Green Forest and that when he be find work in the daytime it mean that he have be undisturbed for a long time ; otherwise he would work only at night .
Paddy saw Lightfoot almost as soon a he step out on the bank .
He keep right on swim with the branch of a poplar-tree until he reach his food pile , which , you know , be in the water .
There he force the branch down until it be hold by other branch already sink in the pond .
This do , he swim over to where Lightfoot be watch .
`` Hello , Lightfoot ! ''
he exclaim .
`` You be look handsomer than ever .
How be you feel these fine autumn day ? ''
`` Anxious , '' reply Lightfoot .
`` I be feel terribly anxious .
Do you know what day this be ? ''
`` No , '' reply Paddy , `` I do n't know what day it be , and I do n't particularly care .
It be enough for me that it be one of the fine day we 've have for a long time . ''
`` I wish I could feel that way , '' say Lightfoot wistfully .
`` I wish I could feel that way , Paddy , but I ca n't .
No , Sir , I ca n't .

The hunter start look for me before Mr. Sun be really out of bed .
At least one hunter do , and I do n't doubt there be others .
I fool that one , but from now to the end of the hunting season there will not be a single moment of daylight when I will feel absolutely safe . ''
Paddy creep out on the bank and chew a little twig of poplar thoughtfully .
Paddy say he can always think good if he be chew something .
`` That 's bad news , Lightfoot .
I 'm sorry to hear it .
I certainly be sorry to hear it , '' say Paddy .
`` Why anybody want to hunt such a handsome fellow a you be , I can not understand .
My , but that 's a beautiful set of antler you have ! ''
`` They be the best I 've ever have ; but do you know , Paddy , I suspect that they may be one of the reason I be hunt so , '' reply Lightfoot a little sadly .
`` Good look be not always to be desire .
Have you see any hunter around here lately ? ''
Paddy shake his Lead .
`` Not a single hunter , '' he reply .
`` I tell you what it be , Lightfoot , let 's be partner for a while .
You stay right around my pond .
If I see or hear or smell anything suspicious , I 'll warn you .
You do the same for me .
Two set of eye , ear and nose be good than one .
What do you say , Lightfoot ? ''
`` I 'll do it , '' reply Lightfoot .
CHAPTER XIV : How Paddy Warned Lightfoot It be a queer partnership , that partnership between Lightfoot and Paddy , but it be a good partnership .
They have be the best of friend for a long time .
Paddy have always be glad to have Lightfoot visit his pond .

Lightfoot himself think the idea a splendid one .
He spend that night browse not far from Paddy 's pond .

It be so quiet and peaceful and beautiful it be hard to believe that hunter with terrible gun be search the Green Forest for beautiful Lightfoot .
But they be , and Lightfoot know that sooner or later one of them would be sure to visit Paddy 's pond .
So , though he rest and take short nap all through that beautiful day , he be anxious .
He could n't help but be .
The next morning find Lightfoot back in the same place .
But this morning he take no nap .
He rest , but all the time he be watchful and alert .

He begin to hope that that day would prove as peaceful a the previous day have be .
Then suddenly there be a sharp report from the farther end of Paddy 's pond .
It be almost like a pistol shot .
However , it be n't a pistol shot .
It be n't a shot at all .
It be the slap of Paddy 's broad tail on the surface of the water .
Instantly Lightfoot be on his foot .
He know just what that meant .
He know that Paddy have see or hear or smell a hunter .
It be even so .
Paddy have hear a dry stick snap .
It be a very tiny snap , but it be enough to warn Paddy .
With only his head above water he have watch in the direction from which that sound have come .
Presently , steal quietly along towards the pond , a hunter have come in view .
Instantly Paddy have bring his broad tail down on the water with all his force .
He know that Lightfoot would know that that mean danger .
Then Paddy have dive , and swim under water , have seek the safety of his house .
He have do his part , and there be nothing more he could do .
CHAPTER XV : The Three Watchers When Paddy the Beaver slap the water with his broad tail , make a noise like a pistol shot , Lightfoot understand that this be mean a a warning of danger .
He be on his foot instantly , with eye , ear and nose seek the cause of Paddy 's warning .
After a moment or two he steal softly up to the top of a little ridge some distance back from Paddy 's pond , but from the top of which he could see the whole of the pond .
There he hide among some close-growing young hemlock-trees .
It be n't long before he saw a hunter with a terrible gun come down to the shore of the pond .

Of course .
There would have be something very wrong with his ear have he fail to hear it .
`` Confound that Beaver ! ''
mutter the hunter crossly .
`` If there be a Deer anywhere around this pond , he probably be on his way now .
I 'll have a look around and see if there be any sign . ''
So the hunter go on to the edge of Paddy 's pond and then begin to walk around it , study the ground a he walk .
Presently he find the footprint of Lightfoot in the mud where Lightfoot have go down to the pond to drink .
`` I think as much , '' mutter the hunter .
`` Those track be make last night .
That Deer probably be lie down somewhere near here , and I might have have a shot but for that pesky Beaver .
I 'll just look the land over , and then I think I 'll wait here awhile .
If that Deer be n't too badly scar , he may come back . ''
So the hunter go quite around the pond , look into all likely hiding-places .
He find where Lightfoot have be lie , and he know that in all probability Lightfoot have be there when Paddy give the danger signal .
`` It 's of no use for me to try to follow him , '' think the hunter .
`` It be too dry for me to track him .
He may not be so badly scar , after all .
I 'll just find a good place and wait . ''
So the hunter find an old log behind some small tree and there sit down .
He could see all around Paddy 's pond .

He be a clever hunter and he know that so long a he do not move he be not likely to be notice by any sharp eye that might come that way .
What he do n't know be that Lightfoot have be watch him all the time and be even then stand where he could see him .
And another thing he do n't know be that Paddy the Beaver have come out of his house and , swim under water , have reach a hiding-place on the opposite shore from which he too have see the hunter sit down on the log .

CHAPTER XVI : Visitors To Paddy 's Pond That hunter be a man of patience .
Also he be a man who understand the little people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows .
He know that if he would not be see he must not move .
So he do n't move .
He keep as motionless a if he be a part of the very log on which he be sit .

They be look and listen to make sure that no danger be near .

It be plain that they felt safe .
Paddy the Beaver be tempt to warn them that they be not as safe a they think , but as long a the hunter do not move Paddy decide to wait .
Now the hunter be sorely tempt to shoot these Ducks , but he know that if he do he would have no chance that day to get Lightfoot the Deer , and it be Lightfoot he want .
So Mr. and Mrs. Quack swam about within easy range of that terrible gun without once suspect that danger be anywhere near .

It be clear that Bobby be quite unsuspicious .
He carry something , but just what the hunter could not make out .
He take it down to the edge of the water and there carefully wash it .
Then he climb up on Paddy 's dam and begin to eat .
You know Bobby Coon be very particular about his food .
Whenever there be water near , Bobby wash his food before eating .

All this Lightfoot saw a he stand among the little hemlock-trees at the top of the ridge behind the hunter .

`` It be because he want to kill me that he do n't shoot at Mr. and Mrs. Quack or Bobby Coon , '' think Lightfoot a little bitterly .
`` What have I ever do that he should be so anxious to kill me ? ''

Mr. and Mrs. Quack contentedly hunt for food in the mud at the bottom of Paddy 's pond .

Time slip away .
The hunter continue to watch patiently for Lightfoot , and Lightfoot and Paddy the Beaver watch the hunter .
Finally , another visitor appear at the upper end of the pond -- a visitor in a wonderful coat of red .

CHAPTER XVII : Sammy Jay Arrives When Reddy Fox arrive at the pond of Paddy the Beaver , the hunter who be hide there saw him instantly .
So do Lightfoot .
But no one else do .
He approach in that cautious , careful way that he always use when he be hunt .

But the hunter do nothing of the kind .
You see , just a he be get ready to step out from his hiding-place , Sammy Jay arrive .

`` Thief , thief , thief ! ''
scream Sammy , and then look down at Reddy with a mischievous look in his sharp eye .

CHAPTER XVIII : The Hunter Loses His Temper The hunter , hide near the pond of Paddy the Beaver , chuckle silently .
That be to say , he laugh without make any sound .

thief !
thief ! ''
at the top of his lung .

CHAPTER XIX : Sammy Jay Is Modest As soon a the angry hunter with the terrible gun have disappear among the tree of the Green Forest , and Lightfoot be sure that he have go for good , Lightfoot come out from his hiding-place on top of the ridge and walk down to the pond of Paddy the Beaver for a drink .

thief !
thief ! ''

CHAPTER XX : Lightfoot Hears A Dreadful Sound Day after day , Lightfoot the Deer play hide and seek for his life with the hunter who be seek to kill him .
He saw them many time , though not one of them saw him .
More than once a hunter pass close to Lightfoot 's hiding-place without once suspect it .
But poor Lightfoot be feel the strain .
He be grow thin , and he be so nervous that the fall of a dead leaf from a tree would startle him .
There be nothing quite so terrible a be continually hunt .
It be get so that Lightfoot half expect a hunter to step out from behind every tree .
Only when the Black Shadows wrap the Green Forest in darkness do he know a moment of peace .
And those hour of safety be fill with dread of what the next day might bring .
Early one morning a terrible sound ring through the Green Forest and bring Lightfoot to his foot with a startled jump .
It be the baying of hound follow a trail .
At first it do not sound so terrible .
Lightfoot have often hear it before .
Many time he have listen to the baying of Bowser the Hound , a he follow Reddy Fox .
It have not sound so terrible then because it mean no danger to Lightfoot .
At first , a he listen early that morning , he take it for grant that those hound be after Reddy , and so , though startle , he be not worry .
But suddenly a dreadful suspicion come to him and he grow more and more anxious a he listen .
In a few minute there be no longer any doubt in his mind .
Those hound be follow his trail .
It be then that the sound of that baying become terrible .
He must run for his life !
Those hound would give him no rest .
And he know that in run from them , he would no longer be able to watch so closely for the hunter with terrible gun .
He would no longer be able to hide in thicket .
At any time he might be drive right past one of those hunter .
Lightfoot bound away with such leap a only Lightfoot can make .
In a little while the voice of the hound grow fainter .
Lightfoot stop to get his breath and stand trembling a he listen .
The baying of the hound again grow louder and louder .
Those wonderful nose of theirs be follow his trail without the least difficulty .
In a panic of fear , Lightfoot bound away again .
As he cross an old road , the Green Forest rang with the roar of a terrible gun .
Something tore a strip of bark from the trunk of a tree just above Lightfoot 's back .
It be a bullet and it have just miss Lightfoot .
It add to his terror and this in turn add to his speed .
So Lightfoot ran and ran , and behind him the voice of the hound continue to ring through the Green Forest .
CHAPTER XXI : How Lightfoot Got Rid Of The Hounds Poor Lightfoot !
It seem to him that there be no such thing a justice and fair play .
Had it be just one hunter at a time against whom he have to match his wit it would not have be so bad .
But there be many hunter with terrible gun look for him , and in dodge one he be likely at any time to meet another .
This in itself seem terribly unfair and unjust .
But now , add to this be the great unfairness of be trail by hound .
Do you wonder that Lightfoot think of men a utterly heartless ?
You see , he could not know that those hound have not be put on his trail , but have leave home to hunt for their own pleasure .
He could not know that it be against the law to hunt him with dog .
But though none of those hunter look for him be guilty of have put the hound on his trail , each one of them be willing and eager to take advantage of the fact that the hound be on his trail .
Already he have be shoot at once and he know that he would be shoot at again if he should be drive where a hunter be hide .
The ground be damp and scent always lie best on damp ground .
This make it easy for the hound to follow him with their wonderful nose .
Lightfoot try every trick he could think of to make those hound lose the scent .
`` If only I could make them lose it long enough for me to get a little rest , it would help , '' pant Lightfoot , a he pause for just an instant to listen to the baying of the hound .
But he could n't .
They allow him no rest .
He be become very , very tired .
He could no longer bind lightly over fall log or brush , a he have do at first .
His lung ache a he pant for breath .
He realize that even though he should escape the hunter he would meet an even more terrible death unless he could get rid of those hound .
There would come a time when he would have to stop .
Then those hound would catch up with him and tear him to piece .
It be then that he remember the Big River .
He turn towards it .
It be his only chance and he know it .
Straight through the Green Forest , out across the Green Meadows to the bank of the Big River , Lightfoot run .
For just a second he pause to look behind .
The hound be almost at his heel .
Lightfoot hesitate no longer but plunge into the Big River and begin to swim .
On the bank the hound stop and bay their disappointment , for they do not dare follow Lightfoot out into the Big River .
CHAPTER XXII : Lightfoot 's Long Swim The Big River be very wide .
It would have be a long swim for Lightfoot have he be fresh and at his best .
Strange a it may seem , Lightfoot be a splendid swimmer , despite his small , delicate foot .
He enjoy swimming .
But now Lightfoot be terribly tire from his long run ahead of the hound .
For a time he swim rapidly , but those weary muscle grow still more weary , and by the time he reach the middle of the Big River it seem to him that he be not get ahead at all .
At first he have try to swim towards a clump of tree he could see on the opposite bank above the point where he have enter the water , but to do this he have to swim against the current and he soon find that he have n't the strength to do this .
Then he turn and head for a point down the Big River .
This make the swimming easy , for the current help him instead of hinder him .
Even then he could feel his strength leave him .
Had he escape those hound and the terrible hunter only to be drown in the Big River ?
This new fear give him more strength for a little while .
But it do not last long .
He be three fourth of the way across the Big River but still that other shore seem a long distance away .
Little by little hope die in the heart of Lightfoot the Deer .
He would keep on just as long a he could and then , -- well , it be well to drown than to be tear to piece by dog .
Just a Lightfoot felt that he could not take another stroke and that the end be at hand , one foot touch something .
Then , all four foot touch .
A second later he have find solid footing and be stand with the water only up to his knee .
He have find a little sand bar out in the Big River .
With a little gasp of return hope , Lightfoot wad along until the water begin to grow deep again .
He have hop that he would be able to wade ashore , but he saw now that he would have to swim again .
So for a long time he remain right where he be .
He be so tired that he tremble all over , and he be as frightened a he be tire .
He know that stand out there in the water he could be see for a long distance , and that make him nervous and fearful .
Supposing a hunter on the shore he be try to reach should see him .
Then he would have no chance at all , for the hunter would simply wait for him and shoot him a he come out of the water .
But rest he must , and so he stand for a long time on the little sand bar in the Big River .
And little by little he felt his strength returning .
CHAPTER XXIII : Lightfoot Finds A Friend As Lightfoot rest , try to recover his breath , out there on the little sand bar in the Big River , his great , soft , beautiful eye watch first one bank and then the other .

CHAPTER XXIV : The Hunter Is Disappointed How he know he be safe , Lightfoot the Deer Could n't have tell you .

CHAPTER XXV : The Hunter Lies In Wait If ever there be an angry hunter , it be the one who have follow Lightfoot the Deer across the Big River .

CHAPTER XXIX : Mr. And Mrs. Quack Are Startled It be the evening of the day after the closing of the hunting season for Lightfoot the Deer .

Mrs. Quack say so .

CHAPTER XXX : The Mystery Is Solved It be very mysterious .
Yes , Sir , it be very mysterious .
Mr. Quack think so .
Mrs. Quack think so .

CHAPTER XXXI : A Surprising Discovery Probably there be no happier Thanksgiving in all the Great World than the Thanksgiving of Lightfoot the Deer , when the dreadful hunt season end and he be once more back in his beloved Green Forest with nothing to fear .

It seem to him that he could not be happy .

What more could any one ask ?

The day be grow colder and the frosty air make him feel good .

Yes , Sir , it be a footprint .

But this time it be not for the beautiful stranger with the dainty foot .
He have no time to think of her now .
He must first find this newcomer and he mean to waste no time in do it .
CHAPTER XXXV : Lightfoot Is Reckless In his search for the new stranger who have come to the Green Forest , Lightfoot the Deer be wholly reckless .
He no longer steal like a gray shadow from thicket to thicket a he have do when search for the beautiful stranger with the dainty foot .
He bound along , careless of how much noise he make .
From time to time he would stop to whistle a challenge and to clash his horn against the tree and stamp the ground with his foot .
After such exhibition of anger he would pause to listen , hop to hear some sound which would tell him where the stranger be .
Now and then he find the stranger 's track , and from them he know that this stranger be do : just what he have be do , seek to find the beautiful newcomer with the dainty foot .
Each time he find these sign Lightfoot 's rage increase .
Of course it do n't take Sammy Jay long to discover what be go on .
There be little that escape those sharp eye of Sammy Jay .
As you know , he have early discover the game of hide and seek Lightfoot have be play with the beautiful young visitor who have come down to the Green Forest from the Great Mountain .
Then , by chance , Sammy have visit the Laughing Brook just a the big stranger have come down there to drink .
For once Sammy have keep his tongue still .
`` There be go to be excitement here when Lightfoot discover this fellow , '' think Sammy .
`` If they ever meet , and I have a feeling that they will , there be go to be a fight worth see .
I must pass the word around . ''
So Sammy Jay hunt up his cousin , Blacky the Crow , and tell him what he have discover .
Then he hunt up Bobby Coon and tell him .
He saw Unc ' Billy Possum sit in the doorway of his hollow tree and tell him .
He discover Jumper the Hare sit under a little hemlock-tree and tell him .
Then he fly over to the dear Old Briar-patch to tell Peter Rabbit .
Of course he tell Drummer the Woodpecker , Tommy Tit the Chickadee , and Yank Yank the Nuthatch , who be over in the Old Orchard , and they at once hurry to the Green Forest , for they could n't think of miss anything so exciting a would be the meeting between Lightfoot and the big stranger from the Great Mountain .
Sammy do n't forget to tell Paddy the Beaver , but it be no news to Paddy .
Paddy have see the big stranger on the edge of his pond early the night before .
Of course , Lightfoot know nothing about all this .
His one thought be to find that big stranger and drive him from the Green Forest , and so he continue his search tirelessly .
CHAPTER XXXVI : Sammy Jay Takes A Hand Sammy Jay be bubble over with excitement a he fly about through the Green Forest , follow Lightfoot the Deer .
He be so excited he want to scream .
But he do n't .
He keep his tongue still .
You see , he do n't want Lightfoot to know that he be be follow .
Under that point cap of Sammy Jay 's be quick wit .
It do n't take him long to discover that the big stranger whom Lightfoot be seek be do his best to keep out of Lightfoot 's way and that he be have no difficulty in do so because of the reckless way in which Lightfoot be search for him .
Lightfoot make so much noise that it be quite easy to know just where he be and so keep out of his sight .
`` That stranger be nearly as big a Lightfoot , but it be very plain that he do n't want to fight , '' think Sammy .
`` He must be a coward . ''
Now the truth be , the stranger be not a coward .
He be ready and willing to fight if he have to , but if he could avoid fight he mean to .
You see , big a he be , he be n't quite so big a Lightfoot , and he know it .
He have see Lightfoot 's big footprint , and from their size he know that Lightfoot must be big and heavy than he .
Then , too , he know that he really have no right to be there in the Green Forest .
That be Lightfoot 's home and so he be an intruder .
He know that Lightfoot would feel this way about it and that this would make him fight all the harder .
So the big stranger want to avoid a fight if possible .
But he want still more to find that beautiful young visitor with the dainty foot for whom Lightfoot have be look .
He want to find her just a Lightfoot want to find her , and he hop that if he do find her , he could take her away with him back to the Great Mountain .
If he have to , he would fight for her , but until he have to he would keep out of the fight .
So he dodge Lightfoot and at the same time look for the beautiful stranger .
All this Sammy Jay guess , and after a while he grow tire of follow Lightfoot for nothing .
`` I 'll have to take a hand in this thing myself , '' mutter Sammy .
`` At this rate , Lightfoot never will find that big stranger ! ''
So Sammy stop follow Lightfoot and begin to search through the Green Forest for the big stranger .
It do n't take very long to find him .
He be over near the pond of Paddy the Beaver .
As soon a he saw him , Sammy begin to scream at the top of his lung .
At once he hear the sound of snap twig at the top of a little ridge back of Paddy 's pond and know that Lightfoot have hear and understood .
CHAPTER XXXVII : The Great Fight Down from the top of the ridge back of the pond of Paddy the Beaver plunge Lightfoot the Deer , his eye blaze with rage .
He have understand the screaming of Sammy Jay .
He know that somewhere down there be the big stranger he have be look for .
The big stranger have understand Sammy 's scream quite as well a Lightfoot .
He know that to run away now would be to prove himself a coward and forever disgrace himself in the eye of Miss Daintyfoot , for that be the name of the beautiful stranger he have be seek .
He MUST fight .
There be no way out of it , he MUST fight .
The hair on the back of his neck stand up with anger just as do the hair on the neck of Lightfoot .
His eye also blaze .
He bound out into a little open place by the pond of Paddy the Beaver and there he wait .
Meanwhile Sammy Jay be fly about in the great excitement , scream at the top of his lung , `` A fight !
A fight !
A fight ! ''
Blacky the Crow , over in another part of the Green Forest , hear him and take up the cry and at once hurry over to Paddy 's pond .
Everybody who be near enough hurry there .
Bobby Coon and Unc ' Billy Possum climb tree from which they could see and at the same time be safe .
Billy Mink hurry to a safe place on the dam of Paddy the Beaver .
Paddy himself climb up on the roof of his house out in the pond .
Peter Rabbit and Jumper the Hare , who happen to be not far away , hurry over where they could peep out from under some young hemlock-trees .
Buster Bear shuffle down the hill and watch from the other side of the pond .
Reddy and Granny Fox be both there .
For what seem like the long time , but which be for only a minute , Lightfoot and the big stranger stand still , glare at each other .
Then , snort with rage , they lower their head and plunge together .
Their antler clash with a noise that ring through the Green Forest , and both fell to their knee .
There they push and struggle .
Then they separate and back away , to repeat the movement over again .
It be a terrible fight .
Everybody say so .
If they have not know before , everybody know now what those great antler be for .
Once the big stranger manage to reach Lightfoot 's right shoulder with one of the sharp point of his antler and make a long tear in Lightfoot 's gray coat .
It only make Lightfoot fight harder .
Sometimes they would rear up and strike with their sharp hoof .
Back and forth they plunge , and the ground be tear up by their foot .
Both be get out of breath , and from time to time they have to stop for a moment 's rest .
Then they would come together again more fiercely than ever .
Never have such a fight be see in the Green Forest .
CHAPTER XXXVIII : An Unseen Watcher As Lightfoot the Deer and the big stranger from the Great Mountain fought in the little opening near the pond of Paddy the Beaver , neither know or care who saw them .
Each be fill fully with rage and determine to drive the other from the Green Forest .
Each be fight for the right to win the love of Miss Daintyfoot .
Neither of them know that Miss Daintyfoot herself be watch them .
But she be .
She have hear the clash of their great antler a they have come together the first time , and she have know exactly what it mean .
Timidly she have steal forward to a thicket where , safely hidden , she could watch that terrible fight .
She know that they be fight for her .
Of course .
She know it just a she have know how both have be hunt for her .
What she do n't know for some time be which one she want to win that fight .
Both Lightfoot and the big stranger be handsome .
Yes , indeed , they be very handsome .
Lightfoot be just a little bit the big and it seem to her just a little bit the handsomer .
She almost want him to win .
Then , when she saw how bravely the big stranger be fight and how well he be hold his own , even though he be a little small than Lightfoot , she almost hop he would win .
That great fight last a long time .
To pretty Miss Daintyfoot it seem that it never would end .
But after a while Lightfoot 's great size and strength begin to tell .
Little by little the big stranger be force back towards the edge of the open place .
Now he would be throw to his knee when Lightfoot be n't .
As Lightfoot saw this , he seem to gain new strength .
At last he catch the stranger in such a way that he throw him over .
While the stranger struggle to get to his foot again , Lightfoot 's sharp antler make long tear in his gray coat .
The stranger be beat and he know it .
The instant he succeed in get to his foot he turn tail and plunge for the shelter of the Green Forest .
With a snort of triumph , Lightfoot plunge after him .
But now that he be beat , fear take possession of the stranger .
All desire to fight left him .
His one thought be to get away , and fear give him speed .
Straight back towards the Great Mountain from which he have come the stranger head .
Lightfoot follow only a short distance .
He know that that stranger be go for good and would not come back .
Then Lightfoot turn back to the open place where they have fight .
There he throw up his beautiful head , crown by it great antler , and whistle a challenge to all the Green Forest .
As she look at him , Miss Daintyfoot know that she have want him to win .
She know that there simply could n't be anybody else so handsome and strong and brave in all the Great World .
CHAPTER XXXIX : Lightfoot Discovers Love Wonderfully handsome be Lightfoot the Deer a he stand in the little opening by the pond of Paddy the Beaver , his head throw back proudly , a he receive the congratulation of his neighbor of the Green Forest who have see him win the great fight with the big stranger who have come down from the Great Mountain .
To beautiful Miss Daintyfoot , peep out from the thicket where she have hide to watch the great fight , Lightfoot be the most wonderful person in all the Great World .
She adore him , which mean that she love him just as much a it be possible for her to love .
But Lightfoot do n't know this .
In fact , he do n't know that Miss Daintyfoot be there .
His one thought have be to drive out of the Green Forest the big stranger who have come down from the Great Mountain .
He have be jealous of that big stranger , though he have n't know that he be jealous .
The real cause of his anger and desire to fight had be the fear that the big stranger would find Miss Daintyfoot and take her away .
Of course this be nothing but jealousy .
Now that the great fight be over , and he know that the big stranger be hurry back to the Great Mountain , all Lightfoot 's anger melt away .
In it place be a great longing to find Miss Daintyfoot .
His great eye become once more soft and beautiful .
In them be a look of wistfulness .
Lightfoot walk down to the edge of the water and drank , for he be very , very thirsty .
Then he turn , intend to take up once more his search for beautiful Miss Daintyfoot .
When he turn he face the thicket in which Miss Daintyfoot be hide .
His keen eye catch a little movement of the branch .
A beautiful head be slowly thrust out , and Lightfoot gaze again into a pair of soft eye which he be sure be the most beautiful eye in all the Great World .
He wonder if she would disappear and run away a she have the last time he saw her .
He take a step or two forward .
The beautiful head be withdraw .
Lightfoot 's heart sank .
Then he bound forward into that thicket .
He more than half expect to find no one there , but when he enter that thicket he receive the most wonderful surprise in all his life .
There stand Miss Daintyfoot , timid , bashful , but with a look in her eye which Lightfoot could not mistake .
In that instant Light-foot understand the meaning of that longing which have keep him hunt for her and of the rage which have fill him when he have discover the presence of the big stranger from the Great Mountain .
It be love .
Lightfoot know that he love Miss Daintyfoot and , look into her soft , gentle eye , he know that Miss Daintyfoot love him .
CHAPTER XL : Happy Days In The Green Forest These be happy day in the Green Forest .
At least , they be happy for Lightfoot the Deer .
They be the happy day he have ever know .
You see , he have win beautiful , slender , young Miss Daintyfoot , and now she be no long Miss Daintyfoot but Mrs. Lightfoot .
Lightfoot be sure that there be no one anywhere so beautiful a she , and Mrs. Lightfoot know that there be no one so handsome and brave a he .
Wherever Lightfoot go , Mrs. Lightfoot go .
He show her all his favorite hiding-places .
He lead her to his favorite eating-places .
She do not tell him that she be already acquaint with every one of them , that she know the Green Forest quite as well a he do .
If he have stop to think how day after day she have manage to keep out of his sight while he hunt for her , he would have realize that there be little he could show her which she do not already know .
But he do n't stop to think and proudly lead her from place to place .
And Mrs. Lightfoot wisely express delight with all she saw quite a if it be all new .
Of course , all the little people of the Green Forest hurry to pay their respect to Mrs. Lightfoot and to tell Lightfoot how glad they felt for him .
And they really do feel glad .
You see , they all love Lightfoot and they know that now he would be happy than ever , and that there would be no danger of his leave the Green Forest because of loneliness .
The Green Forest would not be the same at all without Lightfoot the Deer .
Lightfoot tell Mrs. Lightfoot all about the terrible day of the hunting season and how glad he be that she have not be in the Green Forest then .
He tell her how the hunter with terrible gun have give him no rest and how he have have to swim the Big River to get away from the hound .
`` I know , '' reply Mrs. Lightfoot softly .
`` I know all about it .
You see , there be hunter on the Great Mountain .
In fact , that be how I happen to come down to the Green Forest .
They hunt me so up there that I do not dare stay , and I come down here think that there might be few hunter .
I would n't have believe that I could ever be thankful to hunter for anything , but I be , truly I be . ''
There be a puzzled look on Lightfoot 's face .
`` What for ? ''
he demand .
`` I ca n't imagine anybody be thankful to hunter for anything . ''
`` Oh , you stupid , '' cry Mrs. Lightfoot .
`` Do n't you see that if I have n't be drive down from the Great Mountain , I never would have find YOU ? ''
`` You mean , I never would have find YOU , '' retort Lightfoot .
`` I guess I owe these hunter more than you do .
I owe them the great happiness I have ever know , but I never would have think of it myself .
Is n't it queer how thing which seem the very bad possible sometimes turn out to be the very best possible ? ''
Blacky the Crow be one of Lightfoot 's friend , but sometimes even friend be envious .
It be so with Blacky .
He insist that he be quite as important in the Green Forest a be Lightfoot and that his doings be quite a interesting .
