I DANNY MEADOW MOUSE LEARNS WHY HIS TAIL IS SHORT Danny Meadow Mouse sit in his doorway and look down the Lone Little Path across the Green Meadows .
Way , way over near the Smiling Pool he could see Old Mother West Wind 's Children , the Merry Little Breezes , at play .
Sammy Jay be sit on a fence post .
He pretend to be take a sun bath , but really he be plan mischief .
You never see Sammy Jay that he be n't in mischief or plan it .
Reddy Fox have trot past an hour before in a great hurry .
Up on the hill Danny Meadow Mouse could just see Jimmy Skunk pulling over every old stick and stone he could find , no matter whose house it might be , and excuse himself because he be hungry and be look for beetle .
Jolly , round , red Mr. Sun be play at hide and seek behind some fleecy white cloud .
All the bird be sing and singing , and the world be happy -- all but Danny Meadow Mouse .
No , Danny Meadow Mouse be not happy .
Indeed , he be very far from happy , and all because his tail be short .
By and by up come old Mr. Toad .
It be a warm day and Mr. Toad be very hot and very , very thirsty .
He stop to rest beside the house of Danny Meadow Mouse .
`` Good morning , Danny Meadow Mouse , '' say old Mr. Toad , `` it 's a fine morning . ''
`` Morning , '' say Danny Meadow Mouse , grumpily .
`` I hope your health be good this morning , '' continue old Mr. Toad , just a if he have n't notice how short and cross Danny Meadow Mouse have answer .
Now old Mr. Toad be very ugly to look upon , but the ugliness be all in his look .
He have the sunniest of heart and always he be look for a chance to help someone .
`` Danny Meadow Mouse , '' say old Mr. Toad , `` you make me think of your grandfather a thousand time remove .
You do indeed .
You look just a he do when he lose the half of his tail and realize that he never , never could get it back again . ''
Danny Meadow Mouse sit up suddenly .
`` What be you talk about , old Mr. Toad ?
What be you talk about ? ''
he ask .
`` Did my grandfather a thousand time remove lose the half of his tail , and be it short then than mine be now ?
Was it , old Mr. Toad ?
And how do he come to lose the half of it ? ''
Old Mr. Toad laugh a funny silent laugh .
`` It 's a long story , '' say old Mr. Toad , `` and I 'm afraid I ca n't tell it .
Go down to the Smiling Pool and ask Great-Grandfather Frog , who be my first cousin , how it happen your grandfather a thousand time remove lose the half of his tail .
But before you go catch three fat , foolish , green fly and take them with you a a present to Grandfather Frog . ''
Danny Meadow Mouse could hardly wait for old Mr. Toad to stop speaking .
In fact , he be in such a hurry that he almost forget his manner .
Not quite , however , for he shout `` Thank you , Mr. Toad , thank you ! ''
over his shoulder a he rush off down the Lone Little Path .
You see his short tail have always be a matter of mortification to Danny Meadow Mouse .
All his cousin in the Mouse family and the Rat family have long , smooth , taper tail , and they have always be a source of envy to Danny Meadow Mouse .
He have felt his queer short tail to be a sort of disgrace .
So when he would meet one of his cousin dance down the Lone Little Path , with his long , slim , taper tail behind him , Danny Meadow Mouse would slip out of sight under the long grass , he be so ashamed of his own little tail .
It look so mean and small !
He have wonder and wonder if the Meadow Mice have always have short tail .
He use to ask everyone who come his way if they have ever see a Meadow Mouse with a long tail , but he have never find any one who have .
`` Perhaps , '' think Danny Meadow Mouse a he hurry down the Lone Little Path , `` perhaps Grandfather Frog , who be very wise , will know why my tail be short . ''
So he hurry this way and he hurry that way over the Green Meadows in search of fat , foolish , green fly .
And when he have catch three , he catch one more for good measure .
Then he start for the Smiling Pool as fast a his short leg would take him .
When finally he reach the edge of the Smiling Pool he be quite out of breath .
There sat Great-Grandfather Frog on his big , green lily pad .
He be blink his great goggle eye at jolly , round , red Mr. Sun .
`` Oh , Grandfather Frog , '' say Danny Meadow Mouse in a very small voice , for you know he be quite out of breath with running , `` Oh , Grandfather Frog , I 've bring you four fat , foolish , green fly . ''
Grandfather Frog put a hand behind an ear and listen .
`` Did I hear someone say ` foolish , green fly ? ' ''
ask Grandfather Frog .
`` Yes , Grandfather Frog , here they be , '' say Danny Meadow Mouse , still in a very small voice .
Then he give Grandfather Frog the four fat , foolish , green fly .
`` What be it that you want me to do for you , Danny Meadow Mouse ? ''
ask Grandfather Frog a he smack his lip , for he know that Danny Meadow Mouse must want something to bring him four fat , foolish , green fly .
`` If you please , '' say Danny Meadow Mouse , very politely , `` if you please , Grandfather Frog , old Mr. Toad tell me that you could tell me how Grandfather Meadow Mouse a thousand time remove lost half of his tail .
Will you , Grandfather Frog -- will you ? ''
`` Chug-a-rum , '' say Grandfather Frog .
`` My cousin , Mr. Toad , talk too much . ''
But he settle himself comfortably on the big lily pad , and this be what he tell Danny Meadow Mouse : `` Once upon a time , when the world be young , Mr. Meadow Mouse , your grandfather a thousand time remove , be a very fine gentleman .
He take a great deal of pride in his appearance , do Mr. Meadow Mouse , and they use to say on the Green Meadows that he spend an hour , a full hour , every day comb his whisker and brush his coat .
`` Anyway , he be very fine to look upon , be Mr. Meadow Mouse , and not the least attractive thing about him be his beautiful , long , slim tail , of which he be very proud .
`` Now about this time there be a great deal of trouble on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest , for some one be steal -- yes , steal !
Mr. Rabbit complain first .
To be sure , Mr. Rabbit be lazy and his cabbage patch have grow little more than weed while he have be mind other folk ' affair rather than his own , but , then , that be no reason why he should lose half of the little which he do raise .
And that be just what he say have happen .
`` No one really believe what Mr. Rabbit say , for he have such a bad name for tell thing which be not so that when he do tell the truth no one could be quite sure of it .
`` So no one pay much heed to what Mr. Rabbit say until Happy Jack Squirrel one day go to his snug little hollow in the big chestnut tree where he store his nut and discover half have be steal .
Then Striped Chipmunk lose the great part of his winter store of corn .
A fat trout be steal from Billy Mink .
`` It be a terrible time , for every one suspect every one else , and no one on the Green Meadows be happy .
`` One even Mr. Meadow Mouse go for a stroll along the Crooked Little Path up the hill .
It be dark , very dark indeed .
But just a he pass Striped Chipmunk 's granary , the place where he store his supply of corn and acorn for the winter , Mr. Meadow Mouse meet his cousin , Mr. Wharf Rat .
Now Mr. Wharf Rat be very big and strong and Mr. Meadow Mouse have for a long time look up to and admire him . ''
` Good evening , Cousin Meadow Mouse , ' say Mr. Wharf Rat , swing a bag down from his shoulder .
` Will you do a favor for me ? '
`` Now Mr. Meadow Mouse felt very much flatter , and a he be a very obliging fellow anyway , he promptly say he would . ''
` All right , ' say Mr. Wharf Rat .
` I 'm go to get you to tote this bag down the Crooked Little Path to the hollow chestnut tree .
I 've get an errand back on top of the hill . '
`` So Mr. Meadow Mouse pick up the bag , which be very heavy , and swing it over his shoulder .
Then he start down the Crooked Little Path .
Half way down he meet Striped Chipmunk . ''
` Good evening , Mr. Meadow Mouse , ' say Striped Chipmunk .
` What be you tot in the bag across your shoulder ? '
`` Now , of course , Mr. Meadow Mouse do n't know what be in the bag and he do n't like to admit that he be work for another , for he be very proud , be Mr. Meadow Mouse .
`` So he say : ` Just a planting of potato I beg from Jimmy Skunk , just a planting of potato , Striped Chipmunk . '
`` Now no one have ever suspect Mr. Meadow Mouse of steal -- no indeed !
Striped Chipmunk would have go his way and think no more about it , have it not happen that there be a hole in the bag and from it something drop at his foot .
Striped Chipmunk pick it up and it be n't a potato .
It be a fat acorn .
Striped Chipmunk say nothing but slip it into his pocket . ''
` Good night , ' say Mr. Meadow Mouse , once more shoulder the bag . ''
` Good night , ' say Striped Chipmunk .
`` No sooner have Mr. Meadow Mouse disappear in the darkness down the Crooked Little Path than Striped Chipmunk hurry to his granary .
Some one have be there and steal all his acorn !
`` Then Striped Chipmunk run to the house of his cousin , Happy Jack Squirrel , and tell him how the acorn have be steal from his granary and how he have meet Mr. Meadow Mouse with a bag over his shoulder and how Mr. Meadow Mouse have say that he be tot home a planting of potato he have beg from Jimmy Skunk .
` And this , ' say Striped Chipmunk , hold out the fat acorn , ` be what fell out of the bag . '
`` Then Striped Chipmunk and Happy Jack Squirrel hurry over to Jimmy Skunk 's house , and , just a they expect , they find that Mr. Meadow Mouse have not beg a planting of potato of Jimmy Skunk .
`` So Striped Chipmunk and Happy Jack Squirrel and Jimmy Skunk hurry over to Mr. Rabbit 's and tell him all about Mr. Meadow Mouse and the bag of potato that drop acorn .
Mr. Rabbit look very grave , very grave indeed .
Then Striped Chipmunk and Happy Jack Squirrel and Jimmy Skunk and Mr. Rabbit start to tell Mr. Coon , who be cousin to old King Bear .
`` On the way they meet Hooty the Owl , and because he could fly softly and quickly , they send Hooty the Owl to tell all the meadow people who be awake to come to the hollow chestnut tree .
So Hooty the Owl fly away to tell all the little meadow people who be awake to meet at the hollow chestnut tree .
`` When they reach the hollow chestnut tree whom should they find there but Mr. Meadow Mouse fast asleep beside the bag he have bring for Mr. Wharf Rat , who have wisely stay away .
`` Very softly Striped Chipmunk steal up and open the bag .
Out fell his store of fat acorn .
Then they wake Mr. Meadow Mouse and march him off to old Mother Nature , where they charge him with be a thief .
`` Old Mother Nature listen to all they have to say .
She saw the bag of acorn and she hear how Mr. Meadow Mouse have say that he have a planting of potato .
Then she ask him if he have steal the acorn .
Yes , Sir , she ask him right out if he have steal the acorn .
`` Of course Mr. Meadow Mouse say that he have not steal the acorn . ''
` Then where do you get the bag of acorn ? '
ask old Mother Nature .
`` When she ask this , Mr. Wharf Rat , who be sit in the crowd of meadow people , get up and softly tiptoe away when he think no one be look .
But old Mother Nature saw him .
You ca n't fool old Mother Nature .
No , Sir , you ca n't fool old Mother Nature , and it 's of no use to try .
`` Mr. Meadow Mouse do n't know what to say .
He know now that Mr. Wharf Rat must be the thief , but Mr. Wharf Rat be his cousin , and he have always look up to him a a very fine gentleman .
He could n't tell the world that Mr. Wharf Rat be a thief .
So Mr. Meadow Mouse say nothing .
`` Three time old Mother Nature ask Mr. Meadow Mouse where he get the bag of acorn , and each time Mr. Meadow Mouse say nothing . ''
` Mr. Meadow Mouse , ' say old Mother Nature , and her voice be very stern , ' I know that you do not steal the acorn of Striped Chipmunk .
I know that you do not even guess that there be steal acorn in that bag .
Everyone else think that you be the thief who cause so much trouble on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest .
But I know who the real thief be and he be steal away as fast a he can go down the Lone Little Path this very minute . '
`` All of the little meadow people and forest folk turn to look down the Lone Little Path , but it be so dark none could see , none but Hooty the Owl , whose eye be make to see in the dark . '' '
I see him ! '
cry Hooty the Owl .
` It 's Mr. Wharf Rat ! ' ''
` Yes , ' say old Mother Nature , ` it 's Mr. Wharf Rat -- he be the thief .
And this shall be his punishment : Always hereafter he will be drive out wherever he be find .
He shall no longer live in the Green Meadows or the Green Forest .
Everyone will turn their back upon him .
He will live on what others throw away .
He will live in filth and there will be no one to say a good word for him .
He will become an outcast instead of a fine gentleman . ' ''
` And you , Mr. Meadow Mouse , in order that you may remember always to avoid bad company , and that while it be a splendid thing to be loyal to your friend and not to tell tale , it be also a very , very wrong thing to shield those who have do wrong when by so do you simply help them to keep on do wrong -- you shall no longer have the splendid long tail of which you be so proud , but it shall be short and stubby . '
`` Even while old Mother Nature be speak , Mr. Meadow Mouse felt his tail grow shorter and shorter , and when she have finish he have just a little mean stub of a tail .
`` Of course he felt terribly .
And while Striped Chipmunk hurry to tell him how sorry he felt , and while all the other little meadow people also hurry to tell him how sorry they felt , he could not be comfort .
So he slip away as quickly a he could , and because he be so ashamed he creep along underneath the long grass that no one should see his short tail .
And ever since that long ago time when the world be young , '' conclude Grandfather Frog , `` the Meadow Mice have have short tail and have always scurry along under cover of the long grass where no one will see them .
And the Wharf Rats have never again live in the Green Meadows or in the Green Forest , but have live on filth and garbage around the home of men , with every man 's hand against them . ''
`` Thank you , Grandfather Frog , '' say Danny Meadow Mouse , very soberly .
`` Now I understand why my tail be short and I shall not forget . ''
`` But it be n't your fault at all , Danny Meadow Mouse , '' cry the Merry Little Breezes , who have be listen , `` and we love you just as much a if your tail be long ! ''
Then they play tag with him all the way up the Lone Little Path to his house , till Danny Meadow Mouse quite forget that he have wish that his tail be long .
II WHY REDDY FOX HAS NO FRIENDS The Green Meadows lay peaceful and still .
Mother Moon , sail high overhead , look down upon them and smile and smile , flood them with her silvery light .
All day long the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind have romp there among the aster and goldenrod .
They have play tag through the cat rush around the Smiling Pool .
For very mischief they have rub the fur of the Field Mice baby the wrong way and have blow a fat green fly right out of Grandfather Frog 's mouth just a his lip come together with a smack .
Now they be safely tuck in bed behind the Purple Hills , and so they miss the midnight feast at the foot of the Lone Pine .
But Reddy Fox be there .
You can always count on Reddy Fox to be about when mischief or good time be afoot , especially after Mr. Sun have pull his nightcap on .
Jimmy Skunk be there .
If there be any mischief Reddy Fox do not think of Jimmy Skunk will be sure to discover it .
Billy Mink be there .
Yes indeed , Billy Mink be there !
Billy Mink be another mischief maker .
When Reddy Fox and Jimmy Skunk be play prank or in trouble of any kind you be certain to find Billy Mink close by .
That be , you be certain to find him if you look sharp enough .
But Billy Mink be so slim , he move so quickly , and his wit be so sharp , that he be not see half so often a the others .
With Billy Mink come his cousin , Shadow the Weasel , who be sly and cruel .
No one like Shadow the Weasel .
Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat come .
They be late , for the leg of Little Joe Otter be so short that he be a slow traveler on land , while Jerry Muskrat feel much more at home in the water than on the dry ground .
Of course Peter Rabbit be there .
Without him no party on the Green Meadows would be complete , and Peter like to be abroad at night even well than by day .
With Peter come his cousin , Jumper the Hare , who have come down from the Pine Forest for a visit .
Boomer the Nighthawk and Hooty the Owl complete the party , though Hooty have not be invite and no one know that he be there .
Each be to contribute something to the feast -- the thing that he like best .
Such an array a Mother Moon look down upon !
Reddy Fox have bring a plump , tender chicken , steal from Farmer Brown 's dooryard .
Very quietly , like a thin , brown shadow , Billy Mink have slip up to the duck pond and -- ala !
Now Mother Quack have one le in her pretty little flock than when a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun go to bed behind the Purple Hills , she have count her baby a they tuck their head under their wing .
Little Joe Otter have be fish and he bring a great fat brother of the lamented Tommy Trout , who do n't mind .
Jerry Muskrat bring up from the mud of the river bottom some fine fresh water clam , of which he be very fond .
Jimmy Skunk steal three big egg from the nest of old Gray Goose .
Peter Rabbit and Jumper the Hare roll up a great , tender , fresh cabbage .
Boomer the Nighthawk say that he be very sorry , but he be on a diet of insect , which he must swallow one at a time , so to save trouble he have swallow them a he catch them .
